--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end

--[[
    LeftRight (ModuleScript)

local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			R3(1);
			R6(1);
			R7(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.3);
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)
	local R9 = elsModule(ELSModel.R9)
	local R10 = elsModule(ELSModel.R10)	
	
	--Front lights
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1)
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)

	--Back lights lights
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1)
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do	
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);
				T9(1);
				T10(1);			
				wait()					
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R6(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));						
				R9(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R10(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));														
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)										
					
				R1(0);
				R2(0);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(0);
				R10(0);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)										
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)											
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)					
					
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);					
				wait(0.15)											
				end
			end)
		end)()
				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T5(1)
		T6(1)
		T7(1)
		T8(1)
		T9(1)
		T10(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)
		R9(1)
		R10(1)	
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern2.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern2 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → ELSPatterns

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local centre = brakelights.Centre;
	local top = brakelights.Top;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
		brakelights.Top.Light.Enabled = false;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local headlightState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = true;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = false;
			wait(0.5);
		end; 
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = (headlightState.Value == true and neonMaterial or smoothMaterial);
		indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = headlightState.Value;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Visor lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Rear lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	--Front pushbar lights
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1)
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)
	
	--Front lower pushbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5)
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6)
	
	--Back lights lights
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1)
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));						
				T9(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));														
				wait(0.12)						
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					F1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));	
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					wait(0.15)						
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(216, 115, 61));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(216, 115, 61));
				R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));														
				wait(0.16)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)										
						
				R1(0);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(0);	
				wait(0.16)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)				
						
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.16)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)				
							
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.16)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)					
			
				end
			end)
		end)()			

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
				wait(0.10)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.055)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.10)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.055)					
					
				V1(1);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.10)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.055)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.10)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);					
				wait(0.055)											
				end
			end)
		end)()
				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T7(1)
		T8(1)
		T9(1)
		T10(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)		
	end
end

		R4(1)

		B2(1)

		B4(1)

		V2(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)		
	end
end

				wait(0.08)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.02)										
						
				R1(0);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(0);	
				wait(0.08)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.02)				
						
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.08)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.02)				
							
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.08)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.02)					
			
				end
			end)
		end)()			

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
				wait(0.07)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.02)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.07)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.02)					
					
				V1(1);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.07)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.02)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.07)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);					
				wait(0.02)											
				end
			end)
		end)()
				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T7(1)
		T8(1)
		T9(1)
		T10(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)		
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_Slicktop_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS Slicktop '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local centre = brakelights.Centre;
	local top = brakelights.Top;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
		brakelights.Top.Light.Enabled = false;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_Slicktop_14_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS Slicktop '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_Slicktop_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS Slicktop '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_Slicktop_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS Slicktop '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local headlightState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = true;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = false;
			wait(0.5);
		end; 
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = (headlightState.Value == true and neonMaterial or smoothMaterial);
		indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = headlightState.Value;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_Slicktop_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_14_Charger/BCSS_Slicktop_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS '14 Charger → BCSS Slicktop '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)
	
	if enabled then

		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)
	local R9 = elsModule(ELSModel.R9)
	local R10 = elsModule(ELSModel.R10)	
	
	--Front lights
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1)
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)

	--Back lights lights
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1)
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do	
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);
				T9(1);
				T10(1);			
				wait()					
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R6(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));						
				R9(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R10(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));														
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)										
					
				R1(0);
				R2(0);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(0);
				R10(0);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)										
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)											
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)					
					
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);					
				wait(0.15)											
				end
			end)
		end)()
				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T5(1)
		T6(1)
		T7(1)
		T8(1)
		T9(1)
		T10(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)
		R9(1)
		R10(1)	
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Visor lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Rear lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	--Front pushbar lights
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1)
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)
	
	--Front lower pushbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5)
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6)
	
	--Back lights lights
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1)
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));						
				T9(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));														
				wait(0.12)						
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					F1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));	
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					wait(0.15)						
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(216, 115, 61));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(216, 115, 61));
				R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));														
				wait(0.16)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)										
						
				R1(0);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(0);	
				wait(0.16)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)				
						
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.16)	
			
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);	
				wait(0.085)				
							
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/TDPatterns/LeftRight.lua ---

--[[
    LeftRight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R8(1)
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.3);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

    Line (ModuleScript)

    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.3);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Crown_Victoria/BCSS_Slicktop_Crown_Victoria/Config/TDPatterns/Right.lua ---

--[[
    Right (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Crown Victoria → BCSS Slicktop Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R5(1);
			R6(1);
			R7(1);
			R8(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R6(1);
			R7(1);
			R8(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R7(1);
			R8(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R8(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R8(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Explorer/BCSS_Explorer_B/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Explorer → BCSS Explorer (B) → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)
	local R9 = elsModule(ELSModel.R9)
	local R10 = elsModule(ELSModel.R10)	
	
	--Front lights
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1)
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)

	--Back lights lights
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1)
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do	
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);
				T9(1);
				T10(1);			
				wait()					
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R6(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));						
				R9(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R10(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));														
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)										
					
				R1(0);
				R2(0);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(0);
				R10(0);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)										
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)											
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(1);			
				wait(0.15)					
					
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
				wait(0.25)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)					
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				V1(0);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.25)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);					
				wait(0.15)											
				end
			end)
		end)()
				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T5(1)
		T6(1)
		T7(1)
		T8(1)
		T9(1)
		T10(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)
		R9(1)
		R10(1)	
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
	end
end

				R1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));	
				R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
				R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));						
				R9(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R10(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));														
				wait(0.045)

				wait(0.045)					
						
				R1(1);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);
				R9(0);

				wait(0.045)					
						
				R1(0);

				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);

				wait(0.045)											
						
				R1(0);
				R2(0);

				R5(1);

				R8(1);
				R9(1);
				R10(0);			
				wait(0.045)							
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
				wait(0.12)						
					
				V1(1);
				V2(1);				
				wait(0.03)					
					
				V1(0);

				V1(1);

				V1(1);
				V2(0);				
				wait(0.12)						
						
				V1(1);
				V2(1);					
				wait(0.03)											
				end
			end)
		end)()
				
		
	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
		T5(1)
		T6(1)
		T7(1)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Explorer/BCSS_Explorer_B/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Explorer → BCSS Explorer (B) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Explorer/BCSS_Explorer_B/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Explorer → BCSS Explorer (B) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Explorer/BCSS_Explorer_B/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Explorer → BCSS Explorer (B) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Explorer/BCSS_Explorer_B/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Explorer → BCSS Explorer (B) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Explorer/BCSS_Explorer_B/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Explorer → BCSS Explorer (B) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;
